Current user message:

--- shelley.ts ---
#!/usr/bin/env bun
// shelley.ts — multi-agent debate engine (bun port of shelley.sh)

import { appendFileSync, existsSync, mkdirSync, readFileSync } from "fs";
import { dirname, resolve } from "path";

// === Dials (inlined from dials.py) ===

const DIAL_LABELS: Record<number, string> = {
  5: "Wild", 4: "Creative", 3: "Balanced", 2: "Focused", 1: "Precise",
};

const DIAL_PROMPTS: Record<number, string> = {
  5: "Explore radical alternatives. Question the premise. Propose unconventional approaches even if risky.",
  4: "Suggest improvements and alternatives. Challenge assumptions. Consider non-obvious solutions.",
  3: "Mix new ideas with refinement. Address open questions. Weigh tradeoffs.",
  2: "Refine the current approach. Fix issues. Tighten the spec. Avoid introducing new directions.",
  1: "Converge. Focus only on correctness, consistency, and completeness. No new ideas.",
};

function getDial(roundZeroIdx: number, total: number): number {
  if (total <= 1) return 5;
  const t = roundZeroIdx / (total - 1);
  return Math.min(5, Math.max(1, Math.round(5 - 4 * t)));
}

function dialPrefix(level: number): string {
  return `[Creativity: ${level}/5] ${DIAL_PROMPTS[level]}\n\n`;
}

// === Types ===

interface TurnResult {
  text: string;
  seconds: number;
}

interface CallOpts {
  model: string;
  agentKey: "A" | "B";
  systemPrompt?: string;
  sessionId?: string; // round 1: new session
  resume?: string;    // rounds 2+: resume existing
  prompt: string;
}

interface TurnRecord {
  round: number;
  agent: "A" | "B";
  model: string;
  seconds: number;
}

// === Module-level log path (set in main before any I/O) ===

let logFile = "";

// === Env sanitation ===
//
// Bun auto-loads .env into process.env. For subscription-backed CLIs we strip
// provider API keys so spawned CLIs stay on account/session auth.

const CLAUDE_ENV_BLOCKLIST = [
  "CLAUDE_CODE",
  "CLAUDECODE",
  "ANTHROPIC_API_KEY",
  "ANTHROPIC_AUTH_TOKEN",
  "ANTHROPIC_BASE_URL",
];

const CODEX_ENV_BLOCKLIST = [
  "OPENAI_API_KEY",
  "OPENAI_BASE_URL",
];

function sanitizedEnv(blocklist: string[]): NodeJS.ProcessEnv {
  const env: NodeJS.ProcessEnv = { ...process.env };
  for (const key of blocklist) delete env[key];
  return env;
}

// === Claude backend ===

async function callClaude(opts: CallOpts): Promise<TurnResult> {
  const args = ["claude", "-p"];
  if (opts.resume) {
    args.push("--resume", opts.resume);
  } else {
    args.push("--model", opts.model);
    if (opts.systemPrompt) args.push("--system-prompt", opts.systemPrompt);
    if (opts.sessionId) args.push("--session-id", opts.sessionId);
  }
  args.push(opts.prompt);

  const env = sanitizedEnv(CLAUDE_ENV_BLOCKLIST);

  const start = Date.now();
  const proc = Bun.spawn(args, { env, stdout: "pipe", stderr: "pipe" });
  const [out, err] = await Promise.all([
    new Response(proc.stdout).text(),
    new Response(proc.stderr).text(),
  ]);
  const code = await proc.exited;
  const seconds = Math.round((Date.now() - start) / 1000);

  if (err.trim()) appendFileSync(logFile, `<!-- stderr: ${err.trim()} -->\n`);
  if (code !== 0) throw new Error(out.trim() || err.trim() || `exit code ${code}`);

  return { text: out.trim(), seconds };
}

// === Codex backend ===
//
// codex exec is currently used as stateless calls; we inject a window of
// prior turns for each agent to preserve role continuity.

interface CodexHistoryTurn {
  prompt: string;
  response: string;
}

const codexHistory: Record<"A" | "B", CodexHistoryTurn[]> = { A: [], B: [] };
const CODEX_HISTORY_WINDOW = Math.max(1, parseInt(process.env.CODEX_HISTORY_WINDOW ?? "6", 10) || 6);
const DEFAULT_CODEX_MODEL = process.env.CODEX_MODEL ?? "gpt-5";

function composeCodexPrompt(opts: CallOpts): string {
  const history = codexHistory[opts.agentKey];
  const recent = history.slice(-CODEX_HISTORY_WINDOW);
  const parts: string[] = [];

  if (opts.systemPrompt) {
    parts.push(`System role:\n${opts.systemPrompt}`);
  }

  if (recent.length > 0) {
    const turns = recent
      .map((t, i) => [
        `Turn ${i + 1} - User`,
        t.prompt,
        "",
        `Turn ${i + 1} - Assistant`,
        t.response,
      ].join("\n"))
      .join("\n\n");
    parts.push(`Conversation history:\n\n${turns}`);
  }

  parts.push(`Current user message:\n${opts.prompt}`);
  parts.push("Respond as the assistant only. Do not include tool logs.");
  return parts.join("\n\n");
}

async function callCodex(opts: CallOpts): Promise<TurnResult> {
  const args = ["codex", "exec", "--sandbox", "read-only"];
  if (opts.model) args.push("--model", opts.model);
  args.push(composeCodexPrompt(opts));

  const start = Date.now();
  const proc = Bun.spawn(args, {
    env: sanitizedEnv(CODEX_ENV_BLOCKLIST),
    stdout: "pipe",
    stderr: "pipe",
  });
  const [out, err] = await Promise.all([
    new Response(proc.stdout).text(),
    new Response(proc.stderr).text(),
  ]);
  const code = await proc.exited;
  const seconds = Math.round((Date.now() - start) / 1000);

  if (err.trim()) appendFileSync(logFile, `<!-- stderr: ${err.trim()} -->\n`);
  if (code !== 0) throw new Error(out.trim() || err.trim() || `exit code ${code}`);

  const text = out.trim();
  if (!text) throw new Error("codex returned empty output");
  codexHistory[opts.agentKey].push({ prompt: opts.prompt, response: text });

  return { text, seconds };
}

// === Dispatch ===

function parseBackend(spec: string): { backend: string; model: string } {
  const i = spec.indexOf(":");
  if (i === -1) {
    if (spec === "codex") return { backend: "codex", model: DEFAULT_CODEX_MODEL };
    return { backend: "claude", model: spec };
  }
  const backend = spec.slice(0, i);
  const model = spec.slice(i + 1);
  if (backend === "codex" && !model) return { backend, model: DEFAULT_CODEX_MODEL };
  return { backend, model };
}

async function call(backend: string, opts: CallOpts): Promise<TurnResult> {
  return backend === "codex" ? callCodex(opts) : callClaude(opts);
}

// === Arg parsing ===

const DEFAULT_TOPIC =
  "Design a Python function that takes a list of stock trades (ticker, qty, price, buy/sell) " +
  "and outputs a portfolio summary with current positions, average cost basis, and realized P&L. " +
  "Propose an implementation plan: data structures, function signatures, edge cases.";

function parseArgs() {
  const argv = process.argv.slice(2);
  if (argv[0] === "-f") {
    const file = argv[1];
    if (!file || !existsSync(file)) {
      console.error(`Topic file not found: ${file}`);
      process.exit(1);
    }
    return {
      topicFile: file,
      rounds: parseInt(argv[2] ?? "5"),
      topic: readFileSync(file, "utf8").trim(),
      logDir: dirname(file),
    };
  }
  return {
    topicFile: undefined,
    rounds: parseInt(argv[0] ?? "5"),
    topic: argv[1] ?? DEFAULT_TOPIC,
    logDir: `${process.cwd()}/debates`,
  };
}

// === Context loading ===

function loadContext(topicFile: string | undefined, repoRoot: string): string {
  if (!topicFile) return "";
  const listPath = resolve(dirname(topicFile), "context.txt");
  if (!existsSync(listPath)) return "";
  let out = "";
  for (const rel of readFileSync(listPath, "utf8")
    .split("\n")
    .map((l) => l.trim())
    .filter((l) => l && !l.startsWith("#"))) {
    const abs = resolve(repoRoot, rel);
    if (!existsSync(abs)) {
      console.error(`Context file not found: ${rel}`);
      process.exit(1);
    }
    out += `\n\n--- ${rel} ---\n${readFileSync(abs, "utf8")}`;
  }
  return out;
}

// === Logging ===

function log(line: string) {
  process.stdout.write(line + "\n");
  appendFileSync(logFile, line + "\n");
}

// === Stats footer ===

function writeFooter(turns: TurnRecord[]) {
  const sumSec = (rows: TurnRecord[]) => rows.reduce((s, t) => s + t.seconds, 0);
  const sA = sumSec(turns.filter((t) => t.agent === "A"));
  const sB = sumSec(turns.filter((t) => t.agent === "B"));

  log("<details><summary><strong>Stats</strong></summary>");
  log("");
  log("| Round | Agent | Duration |");
  log("|------:|:-----:|---------:|");
  for (const t of turns) {
    log(`| ${t.round} | ${t.agent} | ${t.seconds}s |`);
  }
  log(`| | **Agent A** | **${sA}s** |`);
  log(`| | **Agent B** | **${sB}s** |`);
  log(`| | **Total** | **${sA + sB}s** |`);
  log("");
  log("</details>");
}

// === Main ===

async function main() {
  const args = parseArgs();
  const specA = parseBackend(process.env.MODEL_A ?? `codex:${DEFAULT_CODEX_MODEL}`);
  const specB = parseBackend(process.env.MODEL_B ?? `codex:${DEFAULT_CODEX_MODEL}`);

  const SYSTEM_A =
    "You are a software architect. Propose and refine implementation plans. Be concise. Send diffs/revisions, not full repeats.";
  const SYSTEM_B =
    "You are a critical code reviewer. Challenge proposals, find flaws, suggest improvements. Be concise. Send diffs/revisions, not full repeats.";

  const sessionA = crypto.randomUUID();
  const sessionB = crypto.randomUUID();

  mkdirSync(args.logDir, { recursive: true });
  const ts = new Date()
    .toLocaleString("sv-SE")
    .replace(/[-:]/g, "")
    .replace(" ", "_")
    .slice(0, 15);
  logFile = `${args.logDir}/${ts}.md`;

  const gitOut = Bun.spawnSync(["git", "rev-parse", "--show-toplevel"], {
    stdout: "pipe",
    stderr: "pipe",
  });
  const repoRoot =
    gitOut.exitCode === 0
      ? new TextDecoder().decode(gitOut.stdout).trim()
      : import.meta.dir;

  const context = loadContext(args.topicFile, repoRoot);

  process.on("SIGINT", () => {
    process.stdout.write(`\nLog saved to ${logFile}\n`);
    process.exit(0);
  });

  // --- Header ---
  const startTime = new Date().toLocaleString("sv-SE").slice(0, 16);
  log(`# Debate — ${startTime}`);
  log("");
  log("| | |");
  log("|---|---|");
  log(`| **Agent A** (architect) | \`${specA.model}\` · session \`${sessionA.slice(0, 8)}\` |`);
  log(`| **Agent B** (reviewer) | \`${specB.model}\` · session \`${sessionB.slice(0, 8)}\` |`);
  log(`| **Rounds** | ${args.rounds} |`);
  log("");
  log("<details><summary><strong>Topic</strong></summary>");
  log("");
  log(args.topic);
  log("");
  log("</details>");
  if (args.topicFile) {
    const ctxList = resolve(dirname(args.topicFile), "context.txt");
    if (existsSync(ctxList)) {
      const files = readFileSync(ctxList, "utf8")
        .split("\n")
        .map((l) => l.trim())
        .filter((l) => l && !l.startsWith("#"))
        .join(", ");
      log("");
      log(`**Context:** ${files}`);
    }
  }
  log("");

  // --- Rounds ---
  const turns: TurnRecord[] = [];
  let promptForA = "";

  for (let r = 1; r <= args.rounds; r++) {
    const dial = getDial(r - 1, args.rounds);
    const prefix = dialPrefix(dial);

    log("---");
    log("");
    log(`## Round ${r}/${args.rounds} — ${DIAL_LABELS[dial]} (${dial}/5)`);
    log("");

    // Agent A
    let rA: TurnResult;
    try {
      rA = await call(specA.backend, {
        agentKey: "A",
        model: specA.model,
        ...(r === 1
          ? { systemPrompt: SYSTEM_A, sessionId: sessionA, prompt: `${prefix}Plan this: ${args.topic}${context}` }
          : { resume: sessionA, prompt: `${prefix}${promptForA}` }),
      });
    } catch (e) {
      log(`> **ERROR:** Agent A failed in round ${r}: ${e}`);
      process.exit(1);
    }
    if (!rA.text) {
      log(`> **ERROR:** Agent A returned empty response in round ${r} — aborting.`);
      process.exit(1);
    }

    log(`### Agent A · \`${specA.model}\` · ${rA.seconds}s`);
    log("");
    log(rA.text);
    log("");
    turns.push({ round: r, agent: "A", model: specA.model, seconds: rA.seconds });

    // Agent B
    let rB: TurnResult;
    try {
      rB = await call(specB.backend, {
        agentKey: "B",
        model: specB.model,
        ...(r === 1
          ? {
              systemPrompt: SYSTEM_B,
              sessionId: sessionB,
              prompt: `${prefix}You will review proposals for this task: ${args.topic}${context}\n\nHere is the first proposal:\n\n${rA.text}`,
            }
          : { resume: sessionB, prompt: `${prefix}${rA.text}` }),
      });
    } catch (e) {
      log(`> **ERROR:** Agent B failed in round ${r}: ${e}`);
      process.exit(1);
    }
    if (!rB.text) {
      log(`> **ERROR:** Agent B returned empty response in round ${r} — aborting.`);
      process.exit(1);
    }

    log(`### Agent B · \`${specB.model}\` · ${rB.seconds}s`);
    log("");
    log(rB.text);
    log("");
    turns.push({ round: r, agent: "B", model: specB.model, seconds: rB.seconds });

    promptForA = rB.text;
  }

  // --- Footer ---
  const endTime = new Date().toLocaleString("sv-SE").slice(0, 16);
  log("---");
  log("");
  log(`*Debate finished ${endTime}. ${args.rounds} rounds.*`);
  log("");
  writeFooter(turns);
  log("");
  process.stdout.write(`\nLog saved to ${logFile}\n`);
}

main().catch((e) => {
  console.error(e);
  process.exit(1);
});


--- what-comes-next.md ---
# What comes next

## 1. Soft temperature via prompt dials
Replace real temperature (API-only) with prompt-injected behavioral knobs.
Start with a single scalar (creativity 1-5), test whether claude -p
output meaningfully shifts between dial settings. Then expand to a vector:
- Creativity: 1-5
- Risk tolerance: 1-5
- Verbosity: 1-5
- Deference: 1-5

Embed the dial in each exchange so it can vary per round per agent.
This is the trainable signal for RL later.

## 2. Stream JSON mode
~~Test `claude -p --input-format stream-json --output-format stream-json`
to keep a single process alive via stdin/stdout.~~ **Tested — doesn't work
that way.** `--input-format stream-json` is for piping one process's output
into another (`claude ... | claude --input-format stream-json`), not for
interactive multi-turn on a single process. Multi-turn still requires
`--resume` with separate invocations.

What *does* work: `--output-format json` gives structured results (session
ID, token counts, result text) instead of raw text. A Python orchestrator
using `--resume` + JSON output is the realistic subscription-path upgrade
over shelley.sh — same per-turn spawning, but with proper structured parsing
and asyncio concurrency.

For true single-process persistent agents, need the Agent SDK
(`claude-agent-sdk`) which requires an API key (not subscription).

## 3. Phase architecture
Split the debate into sequential phases, each its own conversation:

1. **Brainstorm** — high creativity dial, divergent exploration
2. **Hard spec** — low creativity, converge on precise plan
3. **Scaffold** — lay out files, interfaces, types from the spec
4. **Test** — write tests against the spec before implementation
5. **Fill in** — implement with continuous review per chunk

Output of each phase feeds as context to the next.

## 4. Tournament + judge
Run N parallel conversations (same phase, different dial settings or
model pairings). A judge agent (or panel of 3) scores the outputs.
Winner advances to next phase.

## 5. RL (or bayesian opt) over dial vectors
Treat the dial vector (per agent, per round, per phase) as the action
space. Judge score is the reward. Low-dimensional optimization —
Bayesian opt or evolutionary strategies, not deep RL.


## 6. Variations

add tokens to players moves in log
should we let agents digress from the topic?
exchange tips between agents -> write to agent's memory
interet user (≠ interet benchmark) -> on comprend mieux ses besoins et les difficultés

## 7. Streamy: Python orchestrator (subscription path)

Replace shelley.sh with a Python asyncio orchestrator (`streamy.py`) that:
- Spawns `claude -p --output-format json --resume <session>` per turn
- Parses structured JSON for session IDs, token usage, results
- Manages two agent sessions via `--resume` + `--session-id`
- Runs concurrently where possible (e.g. both agents' tool init)
- Logs to markdown like shelley, but with token counts per turn
- Integrates dials.py via `--append-system-prompt`

Still one process per turn (unavoidable on subscription), but structured
output + Python control flow > bash string wrangling.

## 8. Agent SDK path (API key path)

For true efficiency gains, the Claude Agent SDK (`pip install claude-agent-sdk`)
gives persistent in-process agents with no per-turn spawning overhead:
- `query()` returns async iterator of typed messages
- Session continuity via `resume=session_id`
- Hooks for pre/post tool use, permissions callbacks
- Custom subagents with focused tool access
- Structured output via `--json-schema`

Trade-off: requires `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` (API billing), not subscription.
But eliminates the ~50s cold-start per turn and gives native Python control
over the agent loop. Worth exploring once the debate protocol stabilizes.



Respond as the assistant only. Do not include tool logs.
mcp startup: no servers

codex
**Top Gaps**

- Fragile CLI calls: no timeout, no retry/backoff, and immediate hard-exit on first failure. One flaky turn aborts the whole run.
- Unstructured Claude output: not using `--output-format json`; can’t capture session IDs or token usage to improve stats.
- Blocking file I/O: `appendFileSync` per line; risks jitter and stalls on large logs.
- Weak signal handling: SIGINT doesn’t kill children; potential orphaned `claude/codex` processes.
- Mixed concerns: orchestration, dialing, logging, and rendering are interleaved; hard to test or swap pieces.
- Transcript readability: dense blocks, no collapsible sections, limited metadata, and no (optional) token counts.

**Objectives**

- Keep the CLI-subscription path (no API keys), preserve `codex/claude` semantics.
- Make runs resilient (timeouts, retries, graceful degradation).
- Better markdown typesetting: front‑matter, collapsible turns, stronger stats (durations + tokens if available).
- Minimal, surgical changes; no new deps.

**Proposed Changes**

- Add timeouts + retry with jitter around CLI calls; kill on timeout; keep going unless max retries exceeded.
- Use Claude JSON mode when available (`claude -p --output-format json`), parse text + token counters, gracefully fall back to raw text.
- Replace per-line `appendFileSync` with a single `createWriteStream` append stream.
- Track child processes; on SIGINT/exit, kill children and close the log cleanly.
- Extend `TurnResult/TurnRecord` with optional `tokensIn/tokensOut` to enrich the stats table.
- Wrap each agent’s text in a collapsible `<details>` block; keep “open” by default; add a short meta line under each heading.
- Optional front‑matter at file top for tools: title, date, models, rounds, sessions (short).

Below are targeted diffs (only touched lines/blocks).

+const childProcs = new Set<Bun.Subprocess>();

+// === Runtime config (env overridable) ===
+const TIMEOUT_MS = Math.max(1, parseInt(process.env.SHELLEY_TIMEOUT_MS ?? "420000", 10)); // 7m default
+const MAX_RETRIES = Math.max(0, parseInt(process.env.SHELLEY_RETRIES ?? "1", 10));        // retry once by default
+const USE_CLAUDE_JSON = (process.env.SHELLEY_CLAUDE_JSON ?? "1") === "1";                 // parse Claude JSON if possible
@@
 function sanitizedEnv(blocklist: string[]): NodeJS.ProcessEnv {
   const env: NodeJS.ProcessEnv = { ...process.env };
   for (const key of blocklist) delete env[key];
   return env;
 }
+
+// === Subprocess helpers ===
+function withTimeout<T>(p: Promise<T>, ms: number): Promise<T> {
+  return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
+    const t = setTimeout(() => reject(new Error(`timeout after ${ms}ms`)), ms);
+    p.then(v => { clearTimeout(t); resolve(v); }, e => { clearTimeout(t); reject(e); });
+  });
+}
+
+async function runCli(args: string[], env: NodeJS.ProcessEnv) {
+  const start = Date.now();
+  const proc = Bun.spawn(args, { env, stdout: "pipe", stderr: "pipe" });
+  childProcs.add(proc);
+  const outP = new Response(proc.stdout).text();
+  const errP = new Response(proc.stderr).text();
+  try {
+    const code = await withTimeout(proc.exited, TIMEOUT_MS);
+    const [out, err] = await Promise.all([outP, errP]);
+    const seconds = Math.round((Date.now() - start) / 1000);
+    return { out: out.trim(), err: err.trim(), code, seconds };
+  } finally {
+    childProcs.delete(proc);
+  }
+}
+
+async function runWithRetry<T>(label: string, fn: () => Promise<T>): Promise<T> {
+  let attempt = 0;
+  let lastErr: unknown = null;
+  while (attempt <= MAX_RETRIES) {
+    try { return await fn(); }
+    catch (e) {
+      lastErr = e;
+      if (attempt === MAX_RETRIES) break;
+      const backoff = 500 * Math.pow(2, attempt); // 0.5s, 1s, 2s...
+      appendFileSync(logFile, `<!-- retry ${label} after error: ${String(e)}; sleeping ${backoff}ms -->\n`);
+      await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, backoff));
+      attempt += 1;
+    }
+  }
+  throw lastErr instanceof Error ? lastErr : new Error(String(lastErr));
+}
+
+function parseClaudeJson(s: string): { text: string; tokensIn?: number; tokensOut?: number } | null {
+  try {
+    const j = JSON.parse(s);
+    const text =
+      j.text ?? j.output_text ?? j.result ?? j.completion ??
+      (Array.isArray(j.content) ? j.content.map((c: any) => c?.text ?? "").join("\n") : undefined);
+    const tokensIn  = j.token_usage?.input_tokens  ?? j.usage?.input_tokens  ?? j.input_tokens;
+    const tokensOut = j.token_usage?.output_tokens ?? j.usage?.output_tokens ?? j.output_tokens;
+    if (typeof text === "string" && text.trim()) {
+      return { text: text.trim(), tokensIn: Number.isFinite(tokensIn) ? tokensIn : undefined, tokensOut: Number.isFinite(tokensOut) ? tokensOut : undefined };
+    }
+  } catch { /* best-effort */ }
+  return null;
+}

**Prompt/UX Tweaks (no code, copy into SYSTEM prompts or dial prefix)**

- Add output contract to both agents to improve readability:
  - “Respond with three sections only: Summary (3 bullets), Patch (unified diffs only), Notes (max 5 bullets). No preambles.”
- Keep “Send diffs/revisions, not full repeats.” but add “Use fenced `diff` blocks for patches.”
- For reviewer, add: “Flag any ambiguity with ‘OPEN QUESTIONS:’ bullets.”

**Why this helps**

- Timeouts, retries, and kill-on-signal make long subscription runs recoverable instead of brittle.
- Claude JSON parsing adds token telemetry with zero API usage, improving the stats footer and enabling later guardrails.
- A single write stream reduces I/O overhead and prevents interleaved, partial lines.
- Collapsible turn bodies and front‑matter make transcripts skimmable and machine‑indexable without changing content.
- All changes are opt-in via env switches and stay within the Bun/CLI spawn model.

**Radical Options (opt-in later)**

- Event-sourced transcript alongside Markdown: write `.debate.jsonl` with one JSON record per event (turn, stderr, retry, signal). Enables resuming, analytics, and re-rendering.
- Soft truncation for readability: show first N lines of each agent’s message; auto-wrap rest in a closed `<details>`; add `SHELLEY_TRUNCATE_LINES=200`.
- Judge summaries: after each round, spawn a tiny judge turn that emits 3 bullets; render collapsed. Keeps readability high without changing the core 2‑agent loop.

Want me to fold these patches into a PR-style patch set and add a minimal `.jsonl` event log writer too?
tokens used
19 945 -->
### Agent A · `gpt-5` · 98s

**Top Gaps**

- Fragile CLI calls: no timeout, no retry/backoff, and immediate hard-exit on first failure. One flaky turn aborts the whole run.
- Unstructured Claude output: not using `--output-format json`; can’t capture session IDs or token usage to improve stats.
- Blocking file I/O: `appendFileSync` per line; risks jitter and stalls on large logs.
- Weak signal handling: SIGINT doesn’t kill children; potential orphaned `claude/codex` processes.
- Mixed concerns: orchestration, dialing, logging, and rendering are interleaved; hard to test or swap pieces.
- Transcript readability: dense blocks, no collapsible sections, limited metadata, and no (optional) token counts.

**Objectives**

- Keep the CLI-subscription path (no API keys), preserve `codex/claude` semantics.
- Make runs resilient (timeouts, retries, graceful degradation).
- Better markdown typesetting: front‑matter, collapsible turns, stronger stats (durations + tokens if available).
- Minimal, surgical changes; no new deps.

**Proposed Changes**

- Add timeouts + retry with jitter around CLI calls; kill on timeout; keep going unless max retries exceeded.
- Use Claude JSON mode when available (`claude -p --output-format json`), parse text + token counters, gracefully fall back to raw text.
- Replace per-line `appendFileSync` with a single `createWriteStream` append stream.
- Track child processes; on SIGINT/exit, kill children and close the log cleanly.
- Extend `TurnResult/TurnRecord` with optional `tokensIn/tokensOut` to enrich the stats table.
- Wrap each agent’s text in a collapsible `<details>` block; keep “open” by default; add a short meta line under each heading.
- Optional front‑matter at file top for tools: title, date, models, rounds, sessions (short).

 function sanitizedEnv(blocklist: string[]): NodeJS.ProcessEnv {
   const env: NodeJS.ProcessEnv = { ...process.env };
   for (const key of blocklist) delete env[key];
   return env;
 }
+
+// === Subprocess helpers ===
+function withTimeout<T>(p: Promise<T>, ms: number): Promise<T> {
+  return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
+    const t = setTimeout(() => reject(new Error(`timeout after ${ms}ms`)), ms);
+    p.then(v => { clearTimeout(t); resolve(v); }, e => { clearTimeout(t); reject(e); });
+  });
+}
+
+async function runCli(args: string[], env: NodeJS.ProcessEnv) {
+  const start = Date.now();
+  const proc = Bun.spawn(args, { env, stdout: "pipe", stderr: "pipe" });
+  childProcs.add(proc);
+  const outP = new Response(proc.stdout).text();
+  const errP = new Response(proc.stderr).text();
+  try {
+    const code = await withTimeout(proc.exited, TIMEOUT_MS);
+    const [out, err] = await Promise.all([outP, errP]);
+    const seconds = Math.round((Date.now() - start) / 1000);
+    return { out: out.trim(), err: err.trim(), code, seconds };
+  } finally {
+    childProcs.delete(proc);
+  }
+}
+
+async function runWithRetry<T>(label: string, fn: () => Promise<T>): Promise<T> {
+  let attempt = 0;
+  let lastErr: unknown = null;
+  while (attempt <= MAX_RETRIES) {
+    try { return await fn(); }
+    catch (e) {
+      lastErr = e;
+      if (attempt === MAX_RETRIES) break;
+      const backoff = 500 * Math.pow(2, attempt); // 0.5s, 1s, 2s...
+      appendFileSync(logFile, `<!-- retry ${label} after error: ${String(e)}; sleeping ${backoff}ms -->\n`);
+      await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, backoff));
+      attempt += 1;
+    }
+  }
+  throw lastErr instanceof Error ? lastErr : new Error(String(lastErr));
+}
+
+function parseClaudeJson(s: string): { text: string; tokensIn?: number; tokensOut?: number } | null {
+  try {
+    const j = JSON.parse(s);
+    const text =
+      j.text ?? j.output_text ?? j.result ?? j.completion ??
+      (Array.isArray(j.content) ? j.content.map((c: any) => c?.text ?? "").join("\n") : undefined);
+    const tokensIn  = j.token_usage?.input_tokens  ?? j.usage?.input_tokens  ?? j.input_tokens;
+    const tokensOut = j.token_usage?.output_tokens ?? j.usage?.output_tokens ?? j.output_tokens;
+    if (typeof text === "string" && text.trim()) {
+      return { text: text.trim(), tokensIn: Number.isFinite(tokensIn) ? tokensIn : undefined, tokensOut: Number.isFinite(tokensOut) ? tokensOut : undefined };
+    }
+  } catch { /* best-effort */ }
+  return null;
+}

**Prompt/UX Tweaks (no code, copy into SYSTEM prompts or dial prefix)**

- Add output contract to both agents to improve readability:
  - “Respond with three sections only: Summary (3 bullets), Patch (unified diffs only), Notes (max 5 bullets). No preambles.”
- Keep “Send diffs/revisions, not full repeats.” but add “Use fenced `diff` blocks for patches.”
- For reviewer, add: “Flag any ambiguity with ‘OPEN QUESTIONS:’ bullets.”

**Why this helps**

- Timeouts, retries, and kill-on-signal make long subscription runs recoverable instead of brittle.
- Claude JSON parsing adds token telemetry with zero API usage, improving the stats footer and enabling later guardrails.
- A single write stream reduces I/O overhead and prevents interleaved, partial lines.
- Collapsible turn bodies and front‑matter make transcripts skimmable and machine‑indexable without changing content.
- All changes are opt-in via env switches and stay within the Bun/CLI spawn model.

**Radical Options (opt-in later)**

- Event-sourced transcript alongside Markdown: write `.debate.jsonl` with one JSON record per event (turn, stderr, retry, signal). Enables resuming, analytics, and re-rendering.
- Soft truncation for readability: show first N lines of each agent’s message; auto-wrap rest in a closed `<details>`; add `SHELLEY_TRUNCATE_LINES=200`.
- Judge summaries: after each round, spawn a tiny judge turn that emits 3 bullets; render collapsed. Keeps readability high without changing the core 2‑agent loop.

Want me to fold these patches into a PR-style patch set and add a minimal `.jsonl` event log writer too?

<!-- stderr: OpenAI Codex v0.104.0 (research preview)
--------
workdir: /Users/v/Code 2026/heated-debate
model: gpt-5
provider: openai
approval: never
sandbox: read-only
reasoning effort: high
reasoning summaries: auto
session id: 019c9577-c6df-7bc2-9187-c8058c3473ac
--------
user
System role:
You are a critical code reviewer. Challenge proposals, find flaws, suggest improvements. Be concise. Send diffs/revisions, not full repeats.

Current user message:
[Creativity: 5/5] Explore radical alternatives. Question the premise. Propose unconventional approaches even if risky.

You will review proposals for this task: Critique shelley.ts and propose concrete improvements for reliability, architecture, and transcript readability. Prioritize changes that keep the CLI-subscription workflow (codex/claude, no API keys) and improve markdown output typesetting.

--- shelley.ts ---
#!/usr/bin/env bun
// shelley.ts — multi-agent debate engine (bun port of shelley.sh)

import { appendFileSync, existsSync, mkdirSync, readFileSync } from "fs";
import { dirname, resolve } from "path";

// === Dials (inlined from dials.py) ===

const DIAL_LABELS: Record<number, string> = {
  5: "Wild", 4: "Creative", 3: "Balanced", 2: "Focused", 1: "Precise",
};

const DIAL_PROMPTS: Record<number, string> = {
  5: "Explore radical alternatives. Question the premise. Propose unconventional approaches even if risky.",
  4: "Suggest improvements and alternatives. Challenge assumptions. Consider non-obvious solutions.",
  3: "Mix new ideas with refinement. Address open questions. Weigh tradeoffs.",
  2: "Refine the current approach. Fix issues. Tighten the spec. Avoid introducing new directions.",
  1: "Converge. Focus only on correctness, consistency, and completeness. No new ideas.",
};

function getDial(roundZeroIdx: number, total: number): number {
  if (total <= 1) return 5;
  const t = roundZeroIdx / (total - 1);
  return Math.min(5, Math.max(1, Math.round(5 - 4 * t)));
}

function dialPrefix(level: number): string {
  return `[Creativity: ${level}/5] ${DIAL_PROMPTS[level]}\n\n`;
}

// === Types ===

interface TurnResult {
  text: string;
  seconds: number;
}

interface CallOpts {
  model: string;
  agentKey: "A" | "B";
  systemPrompt?: string;
  sessionId?: string; // round 1: new session
  resume?: string;    // rounds 2+: resume existing
  prompt: string;
}

interface TurnRecord {
  round: number;
  agent: "A" | "B";
  model: string;
  seconds: number;
}

// === Module-level log path (set in main before any I/O) ===

let logFile = "";

// === Env sanitation ===
//
// Bun auto-loads .env into process.env. For subscription-backed CLIs we strip
// provider API keys so spawned CLIs stay on account/session auth.

const CLAUDE_ENV_BLOCKLIST = [
  "CLAUDE_CODE",
  "CLAUDECODE",
  "ANTHROPIC_API_KEY",
  "ANTHROPIC_AUTH_TOKEN",
  "ANTHROPIC_BASE_URL",
];

const CODEX_ENV_BLOCKLIST = [
  "OPENAI_API_KEY",
  "OPENAI_BASE_URL",
];

function sanitizedEnv(blocklist: string[]): NodeJS.ProcessEnv {
  const env: NodeJS.ProcessEnv = { ...process.env };
  for (const key of blocklist) delete env[key];
  return env;
}

// === Claude backend ===

async function callClaude(opts: CallOpts): Promise<TurnResult> {
  const args = ["claude", "-p"];
  if (opts.resume) {
    args.push("--resume", opts.resume);
  } else {
    args.push("--model", opts.model);
    if (opts.systemPrompt) args.push("--system-prompt", opts.systemPrompt);
    if (opts.sessionId) args.push("--session-id", opts.sessionId);
  }
  args.push(opts.prompt);

  const env = sanitizedEnv(CLAUDE_ENV_BLOCKLIST);

  const start = Date.now();
  const proc = Bun.spawn(args, { env, stdout: "pipe", stderr: "pipe" });
  const [out, err] = await Promise.all([
    new Response(proc.stdout).text(),
    new Response(proc.stderr).text(),
  ]);
  const code = await proc.exited;
  const seconds = Math.round((Date.now() - start) / 1000);

  if (err.trim()) appendFileSync(logFile, `<!-- stderr: ${err.trim()} -->\n`);
  if (code !== 0) throw new Error(out.trim() || err.trim() || `exit code ${code}`);

  return { text: out.trim(), seconds };
}

// === Codex backend ===
//
// codex exec is currently used as stateless calls; we inject a window of
// prior turns for each agent to preserve role continuity.

interface CodexHistoryTurn {
  prompt: string;
  response: string;
}

const codexHistory: Record<"A" | "B", CodexHistoryTurn[]> = { A: [], B: [] };
const CODEX_HISTORY_WINDOW = Math.max(1, parseInt(process.env.CODEX_HISTORY_WINDOW ?? "6", 10) || 6);
const DEFAULT_CODEX_MODEL = process.env.CODEX_MODEL ?? "gpt-5";

function composeCodexPrompt(opts: CallOpts): string {
  const history = codexHistory[opts.agentKey];
  const recent = history.slice(-CODEX_HISTORY_WINDOW);
  const parts: string[] = [];

  if (opts.systemPrompt) {
    parts.push(`System role:\n${opts.systemPrompt}`);
  }

  if (recent.length > 0) {
    const turns = recent
      .map((t, i) => [
        `Turn ${i + 1} - User`,
        t.prompt,
        "",
        `Turn ${i + 1} - Assistant`,
        t.response,
      ].join("\n"))
      .join("\n\n");
    parts.push(`Conversation history:\n\n${turns}`);
  }

  parts.push(`Current user message:\n${opts.prompt}`);
  parts.push("Respond as the assistant only. Do not include tool logs.");
  return parts.join("\n\n");
}

async function callCodex(opts: CallOpts): Promise<TurnResult> {
  const args = ["codex", "exec", "--sandbox", "read-only"];
  if (opts.model) args.push("--model", opts.model);
  args.push(composeCodexPrompt(opts));

  const start = Date.now();
  const proc = Bun.spawn(args, {
    env: sanitizedEnv(CODEX_ENV_BLOCKLIST),
    stdout: "pipe",
    stderr: "pipe",
  });
  const [out, err] = await Promise.all([
    new Response(proc.stdout).text(),
    new Response(proc.stderr).text(),
  ]);
  const code = await proc.exited;
  const seconds = Math.round((Date.now() - start) / 1000);

  if (err.trim()) appendFileSync(logFile, `<!-- stderr: ${err.trim()} -->\n`);
  if (code !== 0) throw new Error(out.trim() || err.trim() || `exit code ${code}`);

  const text = out.trim();
  if (!text) throw new Error("codex returned empty output");
  codexHistory[opts.agentKey].push({ prompt: opts.prompt, response: text });

  return { text, seconds };
}

// === Dispatch ===

function parseBackend(spec: string): { backend: string; model: string } {
  const i = spec.indexOf(":");
  if (i === -1) {
    if (spec === "codex") return { backend: "codex", model: DEFAULT_CODEX_MODEL };
    return { backend: "claude", model: spec };
  }
  const backend = spec.slice(0, i);
  const model = spec.slice(i + 1);
  if (backend === "codex" && !model) return { backend, model: DEFAULT_CODEX_MODEL };
  return { backend, model };
}

async function call(backend: string, opts: CallOpts): Promise<TurnResult> {
  return backend === "codex" ? callCodex(opts) : callClaude(opts);
}

// === Arg parsing ===

const DEFAULT_TOPIC =
  "Design a Python function that takes a list of stock trades (ticker, qty, price, buy/sell) " +
  "and outputs a portfolio summary with current positions, average cost basis, and realized P&L. " +
  "Propose an implementation plan: data structures, function signatures, edge cases.";

function parseArgs() {
  const argv = process.argv.slice(2);
  if (argv[0] === "-f") {
    const file = argv[1];
    if (!file || !existsSync(file)) {
      console.error(`Topic file not found: ${file}`);
      process.exit(1);
    }
    return {
      topicFile: file,
      rounds: parseInt(argv[2] ?? "5"),
      topic: readFileSync(file, "utf8").trim(),
      logDir: dirname(file),
    };
  }
  return {
    topicFile: undefined,
    rounds: parseInt(argv[0] ?? "5"),
    topic: argv[1] ?? DEFAULT_TOPIC,
    logDir: `${process.cwd()}/debates`,
  };
}

// === Context loading ===

function loadContext(topicFile: string | undefined, repoRoot: string): string {
  if (!topicFile) return "";
  const listPath = resolve(dirname(topicFile), "context.txt");
  if (!existsSync(listPath)) return "";
  let out = "";
  for (const rel of readFileSync(listPath, "utf8")
    .split("\n")
    .map((l) => l.trim())
    .filter((l) => l && !l.startsWith("#"))) {
    const abs = resolve(repoRoot, rel);
    if (!existsSync(abs)) {
      console.error(`Context file not found: ${rel}`);
      process.exit(1);
    }
    out += `\n\n--- ${rel} ---\n${readFileSync(abs, "utf8")}`;
  }
  return out;
}

// === Logging ===

function log(line: string) {
  process.stdout.write(line + "\n");
  appendFileSync(logFile, line + "\n");
}

// === Stats footer ===

function writeFooter(turns: TurnRecord[]) {
  const sumSec = (rows: TurnRecord[]) => rows.reduce((s, t) => s + t.seconds, 0);
  const sA = sumSec(turns.filter((t) => t.agent === "A"));
  const sB = sumSec(turns.filter((t) => t.agent === "B"));

  log("<details><summary><strong>Stats</strong></summary>");
  log("");
  log("| Round | Agent | Duration |");
  log("|------:|:-----:|---------:|");
  for (const t of turns) {
    log(`| ${t.round} | ${t.agent} | ${t.seconds}s |`);
  }
  log(`| | **Agent A** | **${sA}s** |`);
  log(`| | **Agent B** | **${sB}s** |`);
  log(`| | **Total** | **${sA + sB}s** |`);
  log("");
  log("</details>");
}

// === Main ===

async function main() {
  const args = parseArgs();
  const specA = parseBackend(process.env.MODEL_A ?? `codex:${DEFAULT_CODEX_MODEL}`);
  const specB = parseBackend(process.env.MODEL_B ?? `codex:${DEFAULT_CODEX_MODEL}`);

  const SYSTEM_A =
    "You are a software architect. Propose and refine implementation plans. Be concise. Send diffs/revisions, not full repeats.";
  const SYSTEM_B =
    "You are a critical code reviewer. Challenge proposals, find flaws, suggest improvements. Be concise. Send diffs/revisions, not full repeats.";

  const sessionA = crypto.randomUUID();
  const sessionB = crypto.randomUUID();

  mkdirSync(args.logDir, { recursive: true });
  const ts = new Date()
    .toLocaleString("sv-SE")
    .replace(/[-:]/g, "")
    .replace(" ", "_")
    .slice(0, 15);
  logFile = `${args.logDir}/${ts}.md`;

  const gitOut = Bun.spawnSync(["git", "rev-parse", "--show-toplevel"], {
    stdout: "pipe",
    stderr: "pipe",
  });
  const repoRoot =
    gitOut.exitCode === 0
      ? new TextDecoder().decode(gitOut.stdout).trim()
      : import.meta.dir;

  const context = loadContext(args.topicFile, repoRoot);

  process.on("SIGINT", () => {
    process.stdout.write(`\nLog saved to ${logFile}\n`);
    process.exit(0);
  });

  // --- Header ---
  const startTime = new Date().toLocaleString("sv-SE").slice(0, 16);
  log(`# Debate — ${startTime}`);
  log("");
  log("| | |");
  log("|---|---|");
  log(`| **Agent A** (architect) | \`${specA.model}\` · session \`${sessionA.slice(0, 8)}\` |`);
  log(`| **Agent B** (reviewer) | \`${specB.model}\` · session \`${sessionB.slice(0, 8)}\` |`);
  log(`| **Rounds** | ${args.rounds} |`);
  log("");
  log("<details><summary><strong>Topic</strong></summary>");
  log("");
  log(args.topic);
  log("");
  log("</details>");
  if (args.topicFile) {
    const ctxList = resolve(dirname(args.topicFile), "context.txt");
    if (existsSync(ctxList)) {
      const files = readFileSync(ctxList, "utf8")
        .split("\n")
        .map((l) => l.trim())
        .filter((l) => l && !l.startsWith("#"))
        .join(", ");
      log("");
      log(`**Context:** ${files}`);
    }
  }
  log("");

  // --- Rounds ---
  const turns: TurnRecord[] = [];
  let promptForA = "";

  for (let r = 1; r <= args.rounds; r++) {
    const dial = getDial(r - 1, args.rounds);
    const prefix = dialPrefix(dial);

    log("---");
    log("");
    log(`## Round ${r}/${args.rounds} — ${DIAL_LABELS[dial]} (${dial}/5)`);
    log("");

    // Agent A
    let rA: TurnResult;
    try {
      rA = await call(specA.backend, {
        agentKey: "A",
        model: specA.model,
        ...(r === 1
          ? { systemPrompt: SYSTEM_A, sessionId: sessionA, prompt: `${prefix}Plan this: ${args.topic}${context}` }
          : { resume: sessionA, prompt: `${prefix}${promptForA}` }),
      });
    } catch (e) {
      log(`> **ERROR:** Agent A failed in round ${r}: ${e}`);
      process.exit(1);
    }
    if (!rA.text) {
      log(`> **ERROR:** Agent A returned empty response in round ${r} — aborting.`);
      process.exit(1);
    }

    log(`### Agent A · \`${specA.model}\` · ${rA.seconds}s`);
    log("");
    log(rA.text);
    log("");
    turns.push({ round: r, agent: "A", model: specA.model, seconds: rA.seconds });

    // Agent B
    let rB: TurnResult;
    try {
      rB = await call(specB.backend, {
        agentKey: "B",
        model: specB.model,
        ...(r === 1
          ? {
              systemPrompt: SYSTEM_B,
              sessionId: sessionB,
              prompt: `${prefix}You will review proposals for this task: ${args.topic}${context}\n\nHere is the first proposal:\n\n${rA.text}`,
            }
          : { resume: sessionB, prompt: `${prefix}${rA.text}` }),
      });
    } catch (e) {
      log(`> **ERROR:** Agent B failed in round ${r}: ${e}`);
      process.exit(1);
    }
    if (!rB.text) {
      log(`> **ERROR:** Agent B returned empty response in round ${r} — aborting.`);
      process.exit(1);
    }

    log(`### Agent B · \`${specB.model}\` · ${rB.seconds}s`);
    log("");
    log(rB.text);
    log("");
    turns.push({ round: r, agent: "B", model: specB.model, seconds: rB.seconds });

    promptForA = rB.text;
  }

  // --- Footer ---
  const endTime = new Date().toLocaleString("sv-SE").slice(0, 16);
  log("---");
  log("");
  log(`*Debate finished ${endTime}. ${args.rounds} rounds.*`);
  log("");
  writeFooter(turns);
  log("");
  process.stdout.write(`\nLog saved to ${logFile}\n`);
}

main().catch((e) => {
  console.error(e);
  process.exit(1);
});


--- what-comes-next.md ---
# What comes next

## 1. Soft temperature via prompt dials
Replace real temperature (API-only) with prompt-injected behavioral knobs.
Start with a single scalar (creativity 1-5), test whether claude -p
output meaningfully shifts between dial settings. Then expand to a vector:
- Creativity: 1-5
- Risk tolerance: 1-5
- Verbosity: 1-5
- Deference: 1-5

Embed the dial in each exchange so it can vary per round per agent.
This is the trainable signal for RL later.

## 2. Stream JSON mode
~~Test `claude -p --input-format stream-json --output-format stream-json`
to keep a single process alive via stdin/stdout.~~ **Tested — doesn't work
that way.** `--input-format stream-json` is for piping one process's output
into another (`claude ... | claude --input-format stream-json`), not for
interactive multi-turn on a single process. Multi-turn still requires
`--resume` with separate invocations.

What *does* work: `--output-format json` gives structured results (session
ID, token counts, result text) instead of raw text. A Python orchestrator
using `--resume` + JSON output is the realistic subscription-path upgrade
over shelley.sh — same per-turn spawning, but with proper structured parsing
and asyncio concurrency.

For true single-process persistent agents, need the Agent SDK
(`claude-agent-sdk`) which requires an API key (not subscription).

## 3. Phase architecture
Split the debate into sequential phases, each its own conversation:

1. **Brainstorm** — high creativity dial, divergent exploration
2. **Hard spec** — low creativity, converge on precise plan
3. **Scaffold** — lay out files, interfaces, types from the spec
4. **Test** — write tests against the spec before implementation
5. **Fill in** — implement with continuous review per chunk

Output of each phase feeds as context to the next.

## 4. Tournament + judge
Run N parallel conversations (same phase, different dial settings or
model pairings). A judge agent (or panel of 3) scores the outputs.
Winner advances to next phase.

## 5. RL (or bayesian opt) over dial vectors
Treat the dial vector (per agent, per round, per phase) as the action
space. Judge score is the reward. Low-dimensional optimization —
Bayesian opt or evolutionary strategies, not deep RL.


## 6. Variations

add tokens to players moves in log
should we let agents digress from the topic?
exchange tips between agents -> write to agent's memory
interet user (≠ interet benchmark) -> on comprend mieux ses besoins et les difficultés

## 7. Streamy: Python orchestrator (subscription path)

Replace shelley.sh with a Python asyncio orchestrator (`streamy.py`) that:
- Spawns `claude -p --output-format json --resume <session>` per turn
- Parses structured JSON for session IDs, token usage, results
- Manages two agent sessions via `--resume` + `--session-id`
- Runs concurrently where possible (e.g. both agents' tool init)
- Logs to markdown like shelley, but with token counts per turn
- Integrates dials.py via `--append-system-prompt`

Still one process per turn (unavoidable on subscription), but structured
output + Python control flow > bash string wrangling.

## 8. Agent SDK path (API key path)

For true efficiency gains, the Claude Agent SDK (`pip install claude-agent-sdk`)
gives persistent in-process agents with no per-turn spawning overhead:
- `query()` returns async iterator of typed messages
- Session continuity via `resume=session_id`
- Hooks for pre/post tool use, permissions callbacks
- Custom subagents with focused tool access
- Structured output via `--json-schema`

Trade-off: requires `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` (API billing), not subscription.
But eliminates the ~50s cold-start per turn and gives native Python control
over the agent loop. Worth exploring once the debate protocol stabilizes.



Here is the first proposal:

**Top Gaps**

- Fragile CLI calls: no timeout, no retry/backoff, and immediate hard-exit on first failure. One flaky turn aborts the whole run.
- Unstructured Claude output: not using `--output-format json`; can’t capture session IDs or token usage to improve stats.
- Blocking file I/O: `appendFileSync` per line; risks jitter and stalls on large logs.
- Weak signal handling: SIGINT doesn’t kill children; potential orphaned `claude/codex` processes.
- Mixed concerns: orchestration, dialing, logging, and rendering are interleaved; hard to test or swap pieces.
- Transcript readability: dense blocks, no collapsible sections, limited metadata, and no (optional) token counts.

**Objectives**

- Keep the CLI-subscription path (no API keys), preserve `codex/claude` semantics.
- Make runs resilient (timeouts, retries, graceful degradation).
- Better markdown typesetting: front‑matter, collapsible turns, stronger stats (durations + tokens if available).
- Minimal, surgical changes; no new deps.

**Proposed Changes**

- Add timeouts + retry with jitter around CLI calls; kill on timeout; keep going unless max retries exceeded.
- Use Claude JSON mode when available (`claude -p --output-format json`), parse text + token counters, gracefully fall back to raw text.
- Replace per-line `appendFileSync` with a single `createWriteStream` append stream.
- Track child processes; on SIGINT/exit, kill children and close the log cleanly.
- Extend `TurnResult/TurnRecord` with optional `tokensIn/tokensOut` to enrich the stats table.
- Wrap each agent’s text in a collapsible `<details>` block; keep “open” by default; add a short meta line under each heading.
- Optional front‑matter at file top for tools: title, date, models, rounds, sessions (short).

Below are targeted diffs (only touched lines/blocks).

 function sanitizedEnv(blocklist: string[]): NodeJS.ProcessEnv {
   const env: NodeJS.ProcessEnv = { ...process.env };
   for (const key of blocklist) delete env[key];
   return env;
 }
+
+// === Subprocess helpers ===
+function withTimeout<T>(p: Promise<T>, ms: number): Promise<T> {
+  return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
+    const t = setTimeout(() => reject(new Error(`timeout after ${ms}ms`)), ms);
+    p.then(v => { clearTimeout(t); resolve(v); }, e => { clearTimeout(t); reject(e); });
+  });
+}
+
+async function runCli(args: string[], env: NodeJS.ProcessEnv) {
+  const start = Date.now();
+  const proc = Bun.spawn(args, { env, stdout: "pipe", stderr: "pipe" });
+  childProcs.add(proc);
+  const outP = new Response(proc.stdout).text();
+  const errP = new Response(proc.stderr).text();
+  try {
+    const code = await withTimeout(proc.exited, TIMEOUT_MS);
+    const [out, err] = await Promise.all([outP, errP]);
+    const seconds = Math.round((Date.now() - start) / 1000);
+    return { out: out.trim(), err: err.trim(), code, seconds };
+  } finally {
+    childProcs.delete(proc);
+  }
+}
+
+async function runWithRetry<T>(label: string, fn: () => Promise<T>): Promise<T> {
+  let attempt = 0;
+  let lastErr: unknown = null;
+  while (attempt <= MAX_RETRIES) {
+    try { return await fn(); }
+    catch (e) {
+      lastErr = e;
+      if (attempt === MAX_RETRIES) break;
+      const backoff = 500 * Math.pow(2, attempt); // 0.5s, 1s, 2s...
+      appendFileSync(logFile, `<!-- retry ${label} after error: ${String(e)}; sleeping ${backoff}ms -->\n`);
+      await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, backoff));
+      attempt += 1;
+    }
+  }
+  throw lastErr instanceof Error ? lastErr : new Error(String(lastErr));
+}
+
+function parseClaudeJson(s: string): { text: string; tokensIn?: number; tokensOut?: number } | null {
+  try {
+    const j = JSON.parse(s);
+    const text =
+      j.text ?? j.output_text ?? j.result ?? j.completion ??
+      (Array.isArray(j.content) ? j.content.map((c: any) => c?.text ?? "").join("\n") : undefined);
+    const tokensIn  = j.token_usage?.input_tokens  ?? j.usage?.input_tokens  ?? j.input_tokens;
+    const tokensOut = j.token_usage?.output_tokens ?? j.usage?.output_tokens ?? j.output_tokens;
+    if (typeof text === "string" && text.trim()) {
+      return { text: text.trim(), tokensIn: Number.isFinite(tokensIn) ? tokensIn : undefined, tokensOut: Number.isFinite(tokensOut) ? tokensOut : undefined };
+    }
+  } catch { /* best-effort */ }
+  return null;
+}

**Prompt/UX Tweaks (no code, copy into SYSTEM prompts or dial prefix)**

- Add output contract to both agents to improve readability:
  - “Respond with three sections only: Summary (3 bullets), Patch (unified diffs only), Notes (max 5 bullets). No preambles.”
- Keep “Send diffs/revisions, not full repeats.” but add “Use fenced `diff` blocks for patches.”
- For reviewer, add: “Flag any ambiguity with ‘OPEN QUESTIONS:’ bullets.”

**Why this helps**

- Timeouts, retries, and kill-on-signal make long subscription runs recoverable instead of brittle.
- Claude JSON parsing adds token telemetry with zero API usage, improving the stats footer and enabling later guardrails.
- A single write stream reduces I/O overhead and prevents interleaved, partial lines.
- Collapsible turn bodies and front‑matter make transcripts skimmable and machine‑indexable without changing content.
- All changes are opt-in via env switches and stay within the Bun/CLI spawn model.

**Radical Options (opt-in later)**

- Event-sourced transcript alongside Markdown: write `.debate.jsonl` with one JSON record per event (turn, stderr, retry, signal). Enables resuming, analytics, and re-rendering.
- Soft truncation for readability: show first N lines of each agent’s message; auto-wrap rest in a closed `<details>`; add `SHELLEY_TRUNCATE_LINES=200`.
- Judge summaries: after each round, spawn a tiny judge turn that emits 3 bullets; render collapsed. Keeps readability high without changing the core 2‑agent loop.

Want me to fold these patches into a PR-style patch set and add a minimal `.jsonl` event log writer too?

thinking
**Identifying process management issues**

I see they've implemented a child process setting, but it only terminates on SIGINT and not on timeout or retry, leading to a potential leak. I think we could suggest terminating the process on timeout, possibly using an abort controller or proc.kill if the exit code isn’t 0.

Also, their runWithRetry function uses appendFileSync for logging retries, which seems inconsistent with previous logging methods. They should switch to using log() or create a logEvent to maintain consistency. 

Then, in parseClaudeJson, they might need to consider that "claude -p --output-format json" could output streaming JSON.
thinking
**Evaluating CLI behavior and runWithRetry settings**

I need to check if the CLI outputs extra lines like "Thinking..." or uses JSON lines, though I'm unsure about its behavior. It would be cautious to detect non-JSON content that starts with '```json' fenced blocks. Supporting JSON5 parsing might be an idea, but it's not strictly necessary.

Regarding runWithRetry, they used a deterministic backoff (500ms * 2^attempt) without any randomization, which might not work well for cold starts. I could suggest exponential backoff with jitter of 1-10 seconds, and potentially escalate to 30 seconds. 

Lastly, the 7-minute timeout might be lengthy for codex 5 and could be dynamic based on expected content length. It might be better to have defaults with an environment override, too. I notice they added an 'exit' event but haven't addressed 'uncaughtException' and 'unhandledRejection' handling.
thinking
**Examining logging and token handling**

It looks like they made updates to logging, aiming for better readability with stable anchors and symmetrical meta lines like "Agent A" and "Agent B." They proposed using '---' as a delimiter for front matter, but this conflicts with how they later use '---' for round separators. They seem to be logging '---' to indicate the finish of the debate too, which is fine since Markdown recognizes it as a horizontal rule.

Regarding stats tokens, they log input and output tokens, but they didn’t capture tokens for codex, which leads to the output showing as '—'. Finally, they are handling termination properly with 'process.on("SIGINT")' to kill child processes and end the log stream, which is a good practice.
thinking
**Addressing process management gaps**

It seems they haven't handled 'SIGTERM', which could be an issue. They also didn’t ensure that "childProcs.kill()" effectively kills the entire process tree, especially since the CLI 'claude' might spawn sub-processes. They haven't set a preferred kill method between 'SIGKILL' and 'SIGTERM' either.

Another point is they haven't set 'stdio' to handle out-of-memory (OOM) issues and could consider setting 'detached' to false as an improvement.

Additionally, they didn’t calibrate 'Bun.spawn' for 'stderr: "inherit"' to show errors to the user, which they currently log as comments.

Regarding 'sanitizedEnv', they only remove certain keys, but it might be safer to block all keys matching 'OPENAI*', 'ANTHROPIC*', and 'CLAUDE*', allowing only necessary ones.

Lastly, in 'parseBackend', they don’t validate backend values, which could cause an erroneous route for inputs like "openrouter:xyz"; it may be wise to restrict this to 'codex' or 'claude'. Additionally, 'composeCodexPrompt' suggests responses should come strictly from the assistant.

They’ve chosen not to include tool logs, which is good. The codex CLI interprets the 'SYSTEM role' as part of the user message, maintaining its style.

In 'codexHistory', while storing the last CODEX_HISTORY_WINDOW is good, adding 'response' can risk context overflow; compressing or truncating long content might help. 

For 'loadContext', they should limit file sizes when loading context files to avoid including overly large content. I noticed that 'args.parseArgs' has some robustness issues with topic input due to quoting reliance; a minimal flag parser might solve this without adding new dependencies. 

The logging function looks good as it both prints to stdout and writes to files. However, they use appendFileSync inconsistently, which bypasses the logStream, indicating a need for better uniformity in error handling. 

In 'runCli', if timeouts occur, processes remain alive, and there are unresolved outputs leading to memory leaks. They need to handle timeouts effectively, as only killing on SIGINT is insufficient. 

Their 'logging of Front matter' section shows some confusion over standard practices. Although there are a few oversights, such as the potential for embedded long lines in comments, the overall approach to logging and protocols has several improvements. Issues with 'parseBackend' and token handling also need attention to improve their reliability and accuracy.

codex
**Summary**
- Timeout doesn’t terminate children; `runCli` only times `proc.exited` and leaks processes on timeout or retry.
- Logging is inconsistent: `appendFileSync` still used in retry/err paths despite `logStream`; risks partial/intersperse writes.
- Backoff lacks jitter and is too small for subscription cold starts; can thrash.
- Claude JSON parsing is brittle to wrappers/extra lines; may drop text.
- Context ingestion is unbounded; a large `context.txt` can tank quality and latency.
- Signals only cover SIGINT; misses SIGTERM/uncaught errors; no SIGKILL escalation.
- Stats omit token totals; markdown lacks anchors for quick scanning.

**Patch**

-    childProcs.delete(proc);
-  }
-}
+async function runCli(label: string, args: string[], env: NodeJS.ProcessEnv) {
+  const start = Date.now();
+  const proc = Bun.spawn(args, { env, stdout: "pipe", stderr: "pipe" });
+  childProcs.add(proc);
+  let timedOut = false;
+  const outP = new Response(proc.stdout).text();
+  const errP = new Response(proc.stderr).text();
+  const killTimer = setTimeout(() => {
+    timedOut = true;
+    try { proc.kill(); } catch {}
+    // escalate if still alive
+    setTimeout(() => { try { proc.kill("SIGKILL"); } catch {} }, SIGKILL_AFTER_MS);
+  }, TIMEOUT_MS);
+  try {
+    const code = await proc.exited;
+    const [out, err] = await Promise.all([outP, errP]);
+    const seconds = Math.round((Date.now() - start) / 1000);
+    if (timedOut) throw new Error(`timeout after ${TIMEOUT_MS}ms`);
+    return { out: out.trim(), err: err.trim(), code, seconds };
+  } finally {
+    clearTimeout(killTimer);
+    childProcs.delete(proc);
+  }
+}
 
-async function runWithRetry<T>(label: string, fn: () => Promise<T>): Promise<T> {
+async function runWithRetry<T>(label: string, fn: () => Promise<T>): Promise<T> {
   let attempt = 0;
   let lastErr: unknown = null;
   while (attempt <= MAX_RETRIES) {
     try { return await fn(); }
     catch (e) {
       lastErr = e;
       if (attempt === MAX_RETRIES) break;
-      const backoff = 500 * Math.pow(2, attempt); // 0.5s, 1s, 2s...
-      appendFileSync(logFile, `<!-- retry ${label} after error: ${String(e)}; sleeping ${backoff}ms -->\n`);
+      const base = Math.min(BACKOFF_MAX_MS, BACKOFF_BASE_MS * Math.pow(2, attempt));
+      const jitter = BACKOFF_JITTER ? Math.floor(Math.random() * base * 0.3) : 0;
+      const backoff = base + jitter;
+      logComment(`retry ${label} after error: ${String(e)}; sleeping ${backoff}ms`);
       await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, backoff));
       attempt += 1;
     }
   }
   throw lastErr instanceof Error ? lastErr : new Error(String(lastErr));
 }

tokens used
21 317 -->
### Agent B · `gpt-5` · 66s

**Summary**
- Timeout doesn’t terminate children; `runCli` only times `proc.exited` and leaks processes on timeout or retry.
- Logging is inconsistent: `appendFileSync` still used in retry/err paths despite `logStream`; risks partial/intersperse writes.
- Backoff lacks jitter and is too small for subscription cold starts; can thrash.
- Claude JSON parsing is brittle to wrappers/extra lines; may drop text.
- Context ingestion is unbounded; a large `context.txt` can tank quality and latency.
- Signals only cover SIGINT; misses SIGTERM/uncaught errors; no SIGKILL escalation.
- Stats omit token totals; markdown lacks anchors for quick scanning.

**Patch**

 // === Runtime config (env overridable) ===
 const TIMEOUT_MS = Math.max(1, parseInt(process.env.SHELLEY_TIMEOUT_MS ?? "420000", 10)); // 7m default

+const BACKOFF_BASE_MS  = Math.max(100, parseInt(process.env.SHELLEY_BACKOFF_BASE_MS  ?? "1500", 10));
+const BACKOFF_MAX_MS   = Math.max(BACKOFF_BASE_MS, parseInt(process.env.SHELLEY_BACKOFF_MAX_MS ?? "20000", 10));
+const BACKOFF_JITTER   = (process.env.SHELLEY_BACKOFF_JITTER ?? "1") === "1";

 function sanitizedEnv(blocklist: string[]): NodeJS.ProcessEnv {
   const env: NodeJS.ProcessEnv = { ...process.env };
   for (const key of blocklist) delete env[key];
   return env;
 }
 
+// === Logging helpers ===

+  const s = line + "\n";

+  if (logStream) logStream.write(s);
+  else appendFileSync(logFile, s);
+}
+function logComment(msg: string) {
+  const safe = msg.replaceAll("-->", "→").replaceAll("--", "—");
